class="date" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><p class="slp-text-body2" data-v-fba90f83="" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><!--[-->Published on December 16, 2015<!--]--><!----></p><div class="pill" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><p class="slp-text-body3" data-v-fba90f83="" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><!--[-->2 min read<!--]--><!----></p></div></div><h1 class="slp-text-heading2-bold" data-v-fba90f83="" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><!--[-->Improving Open Development for Everyone<!--]--><!----></h1><p class="slp-text-body1" data-v-fba90f83="" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><!--[-->We want to give everyone that loves GitLab the opportunity to help shape its progress and be empowered to do this effortlessly.<!--]--><!----></p><img onerror="this.setAttribute('data-error', 1)" alt="" data-nuxt-img="" srcset="/_ipx/q_80/images/blog/hero-images/logoforblogpost.jpg 1x, /_ipx/q_80/images/blog/hero-images/logoforblogpost.jpg 2x" src="/_ipx/q_80/images/blog/hero-images/logoforblogpost.jpg" data-v-ff65c6cc=""></div><div class="information" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><!--[--><div class="author" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><img onerror="this.setAttribute('data-error', 1)" alt="Job van der Voort" data-nuxt-img="" srcset="/_ipx/q_80/images/blog/headshots/gitlab-logo-extra-whitespace.png 1x, /_ipx/q_80/images/blog/headshots/gitlab-logo-extra-whitespace.png 2x" src="/_ipx/q_80/images/blog/headshots/gitlab-logo-extra-whitespace.png" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><a href="/blog/authors/Job-van-der-Voort/" data-ga-name="Job van der Voort link" data-ga-location="hero" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><span class="slp-text-body1" data-v-fba90f83="" data-v-ff65c6cc=""><!--[-->Job van der Voort<!--]--><!----></span></a></div><!--]--><!----></div></div><!--]--></div><div class="slp-container" data-v-67a0761e="" data-v-44a5c662=""><!--[--><div class="wrapper" data-v-44a5c662="" data-v-17aee3ce=""><div class="content" data-v-17aee3ce=""><!--[--><div class="body" data-v-44a5c662="" data-v-f357e662=""><p>We want to make it super easy for anyone to contribute to GitLab.</p>
<p>That's why we've changed two things:</p>
<ol>
<li>Feature proposals are now handled in the GitLab projects on GitLab.com.</li>
<li>We've assigned weights to relatively simple <code>Accepting merge requests</code>
issues, to make it clear where new contributors can start.</li>
</ol>
<!-- more -->
<h2 id="feature-proposals" tabindex="-1"><a class="header-anchor" href="#feature-proposals">
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M12.2426 3.75736C11.4615 2.97631 10.1952 2.97631 9.41416 3.75736L7.99995 5.17157C7.60942 5.56209 6.97626 5.56209 6.58573 5.17157C6.19521 4.78105 6.19521 4.14788 6.58573 3.75736L7.99995 2.34314C9.56205 0.781046 12.0947 0.781046 13.6568 2.34314C15.2189 3.90524 15.2189 6.4379 13.6568 8L12.2426 9.41421C11.8521 9.80473 11.2189 9.80473 10.8284 9.41421C10.4379 9.02369 10.4379 8.39052 10.8284 8L12.2426 6.58578C13.0236 5.80473 13.0236 4.5384 12.2426 3.75736Z" fill="#333333"></path><path d="M10.5355 5.4645C10.926 5.85502 10.926 6.48819 10.5355 6.87871L6.87863 10.5356C6.4881 10.9261 5.85494 10.9261 5.46441 10.5356C5.07389 10.145 5.07389 9.51188 5.46441 9.12135L9.12127 5.4645C9.51179 5.07397 10.145 5.07397 10.5355 5.4645Z" fill="#333333"></path><path d="M3.75742 9.41422C2.97637 10.1953 2.97637 11.4616 3.75742 12.2426C4.53847 13.0237 5.8048 13.0237 6.58584 12.2426L8.00006 10.8284C8.39058 10.4379 9.02375 10.4379 9.41427 10.8284C9.8048 11.219 9.8048 11.8521 9.41427 12.2426L8.00006 13.6569C6.43796 15.219 3.9053 15.219 2.3432 13.6569C0.781107 12.0948 0.781107 9.56211 2.3432 8.00001L3.75742 6.5858C4.14794 6.19527 4.78111 6.19527 5.17163 6.5858C5.56216 6.97632 5.56215 7.60948 5.17163 8.00001L3.75742 9.41422Z" fill="#333333"></path></svg>
        </a> Feature Proposals</h2>
<p>In the past we've used Uservoice on feedback.gitlab.com to handle
feature proposals and voting. This has served us well, but we always felt that
we could bring the discussion even closer to the development of GitLab.</p>
<p>As we've introduced <a href="/releases/2015/11/22/gitlab-8-2-released/">Award Emoji with GitLab 8.2</a>
and are extending this to allow
for <a href="https://gitlab.com/gitlab-org/gitlab-ce/issues/3672">sorting, filtering</a>
based on these, we feel now is the time to start migrating
the feature proposals to GitLab.com.</p>
<p>This means that if you want to propose a feature for GitLab CE or EE,
you can now simply create an issue in their respective projects`.
This will allow anyone to vote, comment and discuss this.</p>
<p>This system is even more useful because anyone that has shown interest in the issue will be automatically updated
with the status of the issue once someone starts working on it. In time this will also
reveal areas where we might want to improve GitLab's issue tracker.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://gitlab.com/gitlab-org/gitlab-ce/issues">GitLab CE issues</a></li>
<li><a href="https://gitlab.com/gitlab-org/gitlab-ee/issues">GitLab EE issues</a></li>
</ul>
<h2 id="accepting-merge-requests-with-weight" tabindex="-1"><a class="header-anchor" href="#accepting-merge-requests-with-weight">
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M12.2426 3.75736C11.4615 2.97631 10.1952 2.97631 9.41416 3.75736L7.99995 5.17157C7.60942 5.56209 6.97626 5.56209 6.58573 5.17157C6.19521 4.78105 6.19521 4.14788 6.58573 3.75736L7.99995 2.34314C9.56205 0.781046 12.0947 0.781046 13.6568 2.34314C15.2189 3.90524 15.2189 6.4379 13.6568 8L12.2426 9.41421C11.8521 9.80473 11.2189 9.80473 10.8284 9.41421C10.4379 9.02369 10.4379 8.39052 10.8284 8L12.2426 6.58578C13.0236 5.80473 13.0236 4.5384 12.2426 3.75736Z" fill="#333333"></path><path d="M10.5355 5.4645C10.926 5.85502 10.926 6.48819 10.5355 6.87871L6.87863 10.5356C6.4881 10.9261 5.85494 10.9261 5.46441 10.5356C5.07389 10.145 5.07389 9.51188 5.46441 9.12135L9.12127 5.4645C9.51179 5.07397 10.145 5.07397 10.5355 5.4645Z" fill="#333333"></path><path d="M3.75742 9.41422C2.97637 10.1953 2.97637 11.4616 3.75742 12.2426C4.53847 13.0237 5.8048 13.0237 6.58584 12.2426L8.00006 10.8284C8.39058 10.4379 9.02375 10.4379 9.41427 10.8284C9.8048 11.219 9.8048 11.8521 9.41427 12.2426L8.00006 13.6569C6.43796 15.219 3.9053 15.219 2.3432 13.6569C0.781107 12.0948 0.781107 9.56211 2.3432 8.00001L3.75742 6.5858C4.14794 6.19527 4.78111 6.19527 5.17163 6.5858C5.56216 6.97632 5.56215 7.60948 5.17163 8.00001L3.75742 9.41422Z" fill="#333333"></path></svg>
        </a> Accepting merge requests with weight</h2>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Updated Feb 6, 2017:</strong> <code>up-for-grabs</code> was changed to
<code>Accepting merge requests</code> with weight</p>
</blockquote>
<p>We started using
<a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/user/project/issues/issue_weight.html">issue weight</a>
for issues with <code>Accepting merge requests</code> label to make finding
low-hanging fruits much easier. Now anyone can help make GitLab better for
everyone.</p>
<p>We will assign weight smaller than five to issues that are not too hard or too
big to work on.
Whether you're a first-time contributor, someone that wants to improve their
Ruby / Javascript / Go or someone that wants to contribute, but doesn't have time
for a big bug fix or feature, these are issues that you should be able to work on.
If you're already good at the languages GitLab uses, but you are new
to the project, these issues are perfect for you as well.</p>
<p>Have a look at the <a href="https://gitlab.com/gitlab-org/gitlab/-/issues?label_name%5B%5D=Accepting+merge+requests&amp;sort=weight_asc">Accepting merge requests issues for GitLab on GitLab.com</a>
right now. We will add more over time.</p>
<p>Please follow our <a href="https://gitlab.com/gitlab-org/gitlab-ce/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md">the contribution guidelines</a> to help you get started.</p>
<h2 id="how-can-we-make-it-easier%3F" tabindex="-1"><a class="header-anchor" href="#how-can-we-make-it-easier%3F">
          <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M12.2426 3.75736C11.4615 2.97631 10.1952 2.97631 9.41416 3.75736L7.99995 5.17157C7.60942 5.56209 6.97626 5.56209 6.58573 5.17157C6.19521 4.78105 6.19521 4.14788 6.58573 3.75736L7.99995 2.34314C9.56205 0.781046 12.0947 0.781046 13.6568 2.34314C15.2189 3.90524 15.2189 6.4379 13.6568 8L12.2426 9.41421C11.8521 9.80473 11.2189 9.80473 10.8284 9.41421C10.4379 9.02369 10.4379 8.39052 10.8284 8L12.2426 6.58578C13.0236 5.80473 13.0236 4.5384 12.2426 3.75736Z" fill="#333333"></path><path d="M10.5355 5.4645C10.926 5.85502 10.926 6.48819 10.5355 6.87871L6.87863 10.5356C6.4881 10.9261 5.85494 10.9261 5.46441 10.5356C5.07389 10.145 5.07389 9.51188 5.46441 9.12135L9.12127 5.4645C9.51179 5.07397 10.145 5.07397 10.5355 5.4645Z" fill="#333333"></path><path d="M3.75742 9.41422C2.97637 10.1953 2.97637 11.4616 3.75742 12.2426C4.53847 13.0237 5.8048 13.0237 6.58584 12.2426L8.00006 10.8284C8.39058 10.4379 9.02375 10.4379 9.41427 10.8284C9.8048 11.219 9.8048 11.8521 9.41427 12.2426L8.00006 13.6569C6.43796 15.219 3.9053 15.219 2.3432 13.6569C0.781107 12.0948 0.781107 9.56211 2.3432 8.00001L3.75742 6.5858C4.14794 6.19527 4.78111 6.19527 5.17163 6.5858C5.56216 6.97632 5.56215 7.60948 5.17163 8.00001L3.75742 9.41422Z" fill="#333333"></path></svg>
        </a> How can we make it easier?</h2>
<p>We want to give everyone that loves GitLab the opportunity to help shape its progress and be empowered to do this effortlessly.</p>
<p>How can we make this easier for you? We'd love to hear it in the comments.</p>
